    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_79b6db06-5e17-4de0-bc38-266aa4a3561e'

  <span id="freeText8071559100190199432" style="display:none">Can be read as a <b>standalone</b>.<br /><br />If you’re looking for a story about a good, humble girl, who’s been hurt by someone she thought she could trust, only to find out she’s not as vulnerable as she thought she was and discovers an empowering side of herself that falls in love with the guy who helps her find that self, blah, blah, blah...then you’re gonna’ hate my story.<br /><br />Because mine is not the story you read every time you bend back the cover of the latest trend novel. It’s not the “I can do anything, now that I’ve found you/I’m misunderstood but one day you’ll find me irresistible because of it” tale. Why? Because, if I was being honest with you, I’m a complete witch. There’s nothing redeeming about me. I’m a friend using, drug abusing, sex addict from Los Angeles. I’m every girlfriend’s worst nightmare and every boy’s fantasy.<br /><br />I’m Sophie Price...And this is the story about how I went from the world’s most envied girl to the girl no one wanted around and why I wouldn’t trade it for anything in the world.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12920083335953196507"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403067i/783970._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403067i/783971.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/> <b> STRUCK. SPEECHLESS. </b><br/><br/><b> This book took me on a beautiful journey. It moved me, took my breath away and kept me up all night. It was a well-written, powerful, and deeply moving YA story that absolutely broke the mold and was unlike anything I’d ever read. It blew me away! READ IT! </b><br/><br/>This is not your typical romance novel where girl meets boy and they just fall in love. Yes, this book has a beautiful love story, but its also about so. much. more.<br/><br/>Its about learning the true value of life, about the pr</span>
  <span id="freeText12920083335953196507" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403067i/783970._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403067i/783971.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b> STRUCK. SPEECHLESS. </b><br><br><b> This book took me on a beautiful journey. It moved me, took my breath away and kept me up all night. It was a well-written, powerful, and deeply moving YA story that absolutely broke the mold and was unlike anything I’d ever read. It blew me away! READ IT! </b><br><br>This is not your typical romance novel where girl meets boy and they just fall in love. Yes, this book has a beautiful love story, but its also about so. much. more.<br><br>Its about learning the true value of life, about the price of ignorance, the weight of a self-less action, and the beauty of love.<br><br>This was one of those wonderful books that came to my attention very suddenly about 2 weeks ago. Literally, my inbox was full of glowing recommendations for it and I just knew that I had to drop everything and read it. Best decision I ever made!! Something about the idea of it just made my heart race. I swear I had butterflies even before I started reading.<br><br><b> It literally kept me up reading until 5:00 AM. I kept telling myself I was going to put it down and finish it the next day but I could. not. stop. turning. the. pages. </b><br><br>Hmmm, so what’s it about? Its about Sophie Price.<br><br>Sophie Price is vain. She is spoiled, filthy rich, with work obsessed parents who care only about the ‘appearance’ of a healthy family. She is hurt and angry on the inside. She uses, manipulates and discards friends, boys, everyone. She takes drugs, parties hard, and finds that she just can’t break out of the mold.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “Freedom is just that. Absolutely no restrictions. I abandoned myself to every whim I felt. Every want I fulfilled and every disire was quenched. I wanted for nothing.<br><br>Except attention.” </b> </i> </blockquote><br><br>But everything changes the night her party is crashed by cops and, being on her second drug offence, her father arranges to have her sentenced to six months volunteer work at an orphanage in Uganda.<br><br>Scared out of her mind, thrown into a completely opposite life from anything she’s ever known, she is faced with a whole new world that will change her for ever.<br><br>The whole book is told through Sophie’s eyes and despite my love for alternating POVs, I found that this worked perfectly for the story. She was a very intriguing character who, despite her flaws and behavior, was not a ditz or shallow or stupid. She had simply taken several of the wrong turns in life and also, despite the wealth and opulence she grew up around, was deeply affected by the lack of familial love in her life. She wasn’t abused or anything. But this book really shows the damage that comes from a simple lack of care and love. It brought a whole new meaning to her vanity. Her looks meant everything to her because it brought her adoration from everyone, which was the closest thing she had ever come to love.<br><br><blockquote> <i> “I stood in front of the mirror and took a good hard look. I was as bare as I could make myself, no make up with wet, stringy hair. I hated to look at myself in this state. I didn’t feel real. I felt too exposed and that made me exceedingly nervous, but I made myself look that morning. I memorized that girl. That girl was the real me. Frightened. Worthless. A terrible friend. Terrible daughter. Well educated but so limited in ideas worth having. Beautiful yet repulsive… And finally honest.” </i> </blockquote><br><br>Fisher Amelie did a phenomenal job of instantly transporting you into Sophie’s life. I was right there with her every page of the book. I smiled, laughed, cried a little, fell in love, and felt her growth every step of the way.<br><br>I did love the book from the start, but the story is told in such a way that the more I read, the more strongly I connected to the story. My feelings just grew and grew till it just felt like my heart was going to burst.<br><br>Oh, and the guy? Right. Yes, the guy. Ian – or ‘Dingane’ as the kids called him. I literally loved him from his first line. Their first meeting was just SO powerful. I. FELT. It.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “It was like my body knew instantly that he was mine and that I was his.” </b> </i> </blockquote><br><br>He was take-your-breath-away gorgeous. Blunt. Honest. And saw right through her. And the more we learned about his back story too, the more I loved him…. oh, and he cleared the bugs for her!! When you read the scene, I promise it’ll melt your heart a little ;)<br><br>About Uganda and the orphanage. *deep breath*. Ok. I am mostly aware what is happening in the world. I read the news. I see the headlines and the pictures. But this was different. So. So. Different. This brought the horrors of what was going on to light in a way I can’t even tell you. My heart broke into a million pieces for those kids. The word “horrors” seems too gentle for what I mean. I don’t think there is a word strong enough :(<br><br>My heart bled for those beautiful innocent children who had everything but their lives and their spirit so cruelly and heartlessly stolen from them and yet still sang songs every morning, smiled and found the beauty in life.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “And what is there to be joyful about?”… Another burst of silent tears streamed down.<br><br>“Life, Sophie. They still live. They breathe, they love each other, they find joy in the world around them for no other reason than because they are children. They are resiliant. They will always rise above. Always.” </b> </i> </blockquote><br><br>I loved watching how Sophie, who had never known real love, grew, changed, and opened every part of heart to these kids and to their cause.<br><br>I loved watching her and Ian/Dingane fall in love. Ohhh their chemistry was palatable. It wasn’t a head-over-heels-at-first-sight thing, but it sizzled. I’ve said this before, but <b> I. Felt. It. </b><br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “It’ll be all right,” Ian assured me.<br><br>“How do you know?” I asked when he revved the engine.<br><br>“I don’t,” he said, “but I’ll protect you.” </b> </i> </blockquote><br><br>Their first kiss was seriously one of the best I’ve ever read. I squeed out loud!!!!! The gun lesson *fans self*… and that second last scene! *shivers* Yeah, I loved him. Completely.<br><br>I kept alternating between smiling and being near tears. Every part of the story wormed its way into my heart.<br><br>In the interest of full openness, I’ll say there were a few typos here and there, one or two moments of plot or dialogue that gave me squinty eyes, and despite there being an epilogue, I maybe might have wanted just a wee bit <i> more </i> at the end. But truly, it made no difference. The story was incredible so it didn’t affect my enjoyment of it.<br><br>This is a completely YA story – by that I mean the characters are younger than 20 and there is no sex in the book. But its the kind of beautifully written YA that makes even something as simple and subtle as just a shared glance give you epic butterflies, take your breath away and make your heart just race.<br><br>The story was heart breaking, exciting, beautiful, powerful, and thrilling. There were no dull or slow moments. Ever. There was always something new. Something happening. I was drawn completely into every part of the story. And its one that I won’t forget.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “I’m so deep there’s no getting out for me. You own me, you know?” </b></i>  </blockquote><br><br>This book took me on a beautiful journey. Seriously one of the best books I’ve read in a while.<br><br>Guys, this is a must-read!!<br><br>Oh, and yes, there is a HEA :)<br><br>Casting for Ian and Sophie (also the pic above):<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403067i/783972.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403067i/783973._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u> <b> Official Blurb </b></u>  (I’m including this because it was a big part of what sold me on the book):<br><br><i> If you’re looking for a story about a good, humble girl, who’s been hurt by someone she thought she could trust, only to find out she’s not as vulnerable as she thought she was and discovers an empowering side of herself that falls in love with the guy who helps her find that self, blah, blah, blah…then you’re gonna’ hate my story.<br><br>Because mine is not the story you read every time you bend back the cover of the latest trend novel. It’s not the “I can do anything, now that I’ve found you/I’m misunderstood but one day you’ll find me irresistible because of it” tale. Why? Because, if I was being honest with you, I’m a complete witch. There’s nothing redeeming about me. I’m a friend using, drug abusing, sex addict from Los Angeles. I’m every girlfriend’s worst nightmare and every boy’s fantasy.<br><br>I’m Sophie Price…And this is the story about how I went from the world’s most envied girl to the girl no one wanted around and why I wouldn’t trade it for anything in the world. </i><br><br><b> **NEW COVER ALERT** This book now has a new cover. I’ve posted the old cover at the bottom of the review just for reference.<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403067i/783974._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="12920083335953196507" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer487087537" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11525832332941525022"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402274ra/781758.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> <i> You're so vain...<br/>I bet you think this book is about you, don't you? Don't you? </i> </b><br/><br/>NUH-UH! WRONG!<br/>This isn't about you...<br/><br/>This is about her royalty,<br/><b> <u> SOPHIE PRICE. </u></b> <br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/><i> Who the hell is Sophie Price?! </i><br/>Okay, let me tell you.<br/><br/>She is...<br/><b> *SUPER RICH. GORGEOUS. FLAWLESS! </b><br/>--> <u> Every guy wants her. Every girl wants to be her. </u><br/><br/>Aside from that, she is also:<br/><b> *QUEEN BEE.<br/>*MANIPULATIVE LITTLE BITCH.<br/>*SPOILED, REPULSIVE BRAT<br/>*VICIOUS.<br/>*VAIN VAIN VAIN!!! </b><br/><u> What Sophie wants, Sophie gets. </u><br/>She has people tendin</span>
  <span id="freeText11525832332941525022" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402274ra/781758.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> <i> You're so vain...<br>I bet you think this book is about you, don't you? Don't you? </i> </b><br><br>NUH-UH! WRONG!<br>This isn't about you...<br><br>This is about her royalty,<br><b> <u> SOPHIE PRICE. </u></b> <br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><i> Who the hell is Sophie Price?! </i><br>Okay, let me tell you.<br><br>She is...<br><b> *SUPER RICH. GORGEOUS. FLAWLESS! </b><br>--&gt; <u> Every guy wants her. Every girl wants to be her. </u><br><br>Aside from that, she is also:<br><b> *QUEEN BEE.<br>*MANIPULATIVE LITTLE BITCH.<br>*SPOILED, REPULSIVE BRAT<br>*VICIOUS.<br>*VAIN VAIN VAIN!!! </b><br><u> What Sophie wants, Sophie gets. </u><br>She has people tending her needs, her wardrobe, hair, makeup, nails, EVERYTHING!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402274i/781760.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> <i> I’m one of the beautiful people. That truly sounds so odd to have to explain, but it’s the truth nonetheless. I’m beautiful, and it’s not because I have a healthy dose of self esteem, though I have plenty of that. It’s obvious in the way I look in the mirror, yes, but even more obvious in the way everyone treats me. I rule this roost because I’m the most wanted by all the guys, and all the girls want to be my friend because of it.<br><br>I was the queen of subtlety. I could play a boy like a concert violinist. I was a master of my craft.<br><br>“My lingerie probably costs more than your entire wardrobe,” I spit out at the short, stocky one who eyed me with disdain.<br></i> </b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402274ra/781761.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>EVIL, isn't she???<br>I swear this girl is full of herself. UGH<br><br>She is always out partying, teasing/making out with different guys (even the ones who have girlfriends), and doing drugs.<br><br><i> Hate her? </i><br><br>NO, DON'T.<br><br><b> <i> “Keep appearances, Sophie Price, and I’ll reward you handsomely,” my father said to me starting at fifteen. </i> </b><br><br><blockquote> <b> ...Every want I fulfilled and every desire was quenched. I wanted for nothing.<br>Except attention. </b> </blockquote><br>There's actually a good person hidden inside that hideous persona.<br><br><b> <u> She just doesn't realize it yet... </u></b> <br><br>But, everything's gonna change and all of her evil doings will come to an end.<br><br>Her misdemeanor has taken its toll on her when she was sentenced six months in an orphanage at Masego, Uganda.<br><br>That's when the REAL story begins...<br><br>From there on, she met different types of people. Lead an unfamiliar life. Entirely DIFFERENT from where she came from. <br><br>Actually, it all started when she first laid eyes on the guy who will be one of the reason for the CHANGE in her...<br><br><b> IAN ABERDEEN </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402274i/781762.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>(<b> NEW BOOK BOYFRIEND ALERT!!! </b> He's actually called Dingane [read as Din-John-E], but I don't like it so I'm gonna stick with Ian. LOL.)<br><br><i> Ian is... </i><br><b> *DROP DEAD GORGEOUS (and oh, he's white). </b> --Not really what Sophie imagined since he's from Africa.<br><b>*SELFLESS. </b> He cares for the kids more than himself. Hell, he cares for everyone and will fight for them.<br>But, most especially, unlike any other guys she'd known, <b> *IAN DESPISES HER! </b><br><br><b> <i> “Yes, I was thinking that you were a spoiled brat who won’t last two seconds here.”<br><br>“Girl, you are the epitome of spoiled. I can smell it in your expensive perfume, in the quality of your ridiculous clothing, in the bracelet wrapped ’round that delicate wrist.” He closed the gap between us and all the air sucked from the room. “You won’t last out here. You’ll stay blind to the environment that surrounds you. You’ll live in your clean, perfect bubble and return to your posh life come six months. You are....you. I know your kind. I’ve seen it all before. You will never wake up. Not really.” </i> </b><br><br>UH OH! THAT'S HARSH. <br>It's like a slap to Sophie's face.<br><br>Because if there's one thing she fears, it's being rejected...<br><br><b> I was my own worst enemy. That was my secret weakness. <u> Rejection. </u> Rejection of any kind, in fact. I hated it more than anything. </b><br><br>That's short lived though. Soon, he will find out that they have more things in common than they've known. Most especially, he will see the <b> REAL </b> Sophie... All new and improved version of her.<br><br><i> What happens next??? </i><br><br>I guess you should find out for yourselves :)<br>So, you know what to do...<br><br><b> <u> READ IT!!! </u> </b><br><br><blockquote> <b> EXHILARATING. AMAZING. WONDERFUL. SMARTLY WRITTEN. BLOODY BRILLIANT!!! </b> </blockquote><br><br>I COULD GO ON AND ON AND ON... <br><br><b> OH.MY.WORD! MY GOODNESS! THIS BOOK MAKES IT TO MY LIST OF THE BEST BOOKS OF 2012!!! </b><br><br>I'm speechless.<br>But, I have a question for y'all:<br><br><b> <u> WHY THE HELL ARE YOU NOT READING THIS ONE YET?! <u> </u></u></b><br><br>Seriously? IT'S THE BEST!!!<br><br>Okay, first of all, that cover is misleading. <u> THIS IS NOT A PARANORMAL ROMANCE BOOK. </u> At first, when I saw the cover, I thought it was, but then I read the blurb, so from there, I knew I just have to read this one! No, not because it's not a PNR book (because I also love PNR), but because I can sense it's gonna be an awesome read. And I wasn't disappointed! It exceeded my expectations. From the first page, I was hooked, line and sinker! <br><br><blockquote> <b> Vanity’s a debilitating affliction. You’re so absorbed in yourself it’s impossible to love anyone other than oneself, leaving you weak without realization of it. It’s quite sad. You’ve no idea what you’re missing either. You will never know real love and your life will pass you by. But you will see. One day you will blink and the haze will dissipate. You’ll discover that what once defined you has wilted into graying hair and wrinkled skin. Frantic, you’ll glance around yourself, in hopes of finding those you swore adored you, but all you will find is empty picture frames. </b> </blockquote><br>I just gave you the prologue. See? Who wouldn't get hooked, right?<br><br>This is actually the first book from Fisher Amelie I've read and I wasn't disappointed at all. I will read all her novels and everything that she'll write.<br>To the author:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402274ra/781763.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book gave me everything. Relatable heroine (not in the sense of her bitchiness, but because she is strong, confident, and somehow, vulnerable. She is definitely genuine. She made it to the list of my favorite heroines). Swoon-worthy hero. A couple everyone will ship. Quotable quotes. Romance. Thriller. Action. And, scenes you can't help but bawl your eyes out. I just can't get over it. The author also mentioned LRA and Joseph Kony (I'm sure most of you guys know him and aware of what he has done. If not, google him or search him on YouTube. There's a documentary about him there that earned a million views). This book taught me the value of life. How to be selfless and appreciate what we have and be happy with it.<br><br>I love the prologue and the epilogue. I fell in love with Ian and Sophie's relationship. How they started off and what they had in the end was absolutely beautiful! I ship them so hard!!! They're so cute together and they compliment each other. I love all their conversations. My hands are itching to type/put/quote their convos and romantic scenes here, but I have to be considerate for the future readers. They sure do have chemistry, it's off the charts! AHHHH! *Swooning and fangirling* I love all the secondary characters as well and how they helped Sophie discover who she really is. They are perfect in their own ways. Okay, I LOVE EVERYTHING ABOUT THIS BOOK. Two thumbs up!!!<br><br>One of my favorite convos between the MCs --&gt; <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ “Classes are cancelled for two days after the kids recover. I’m making an executive decision and I’m going to sleep for both of them.”<br>“As long as I get to sleep with you.”<br>My eyes bugged from my head. “Pardon?” I asked in disbelief.<br>Ian stared at me, eyes wide. “I-I just meant...I meant that, uh, that I also wanted to sleep with you.”<br>I laughed out loud.<br>“I mean, not with you but sleep in my own bed during the time in which you also sleep...in your bed. We’d be asleep in two separate beds. You in yours and me in mine.” One of his hands left the steering wheel and<br>ran the length of his face. “God, I’m deprived.” A quick glance my way. “Of sleep! Deprived of sleep!” His hand slapped the wheel. “God, shut up, Din.”<br>I smiled at him softly. “I got you, Ian.” Boy, do I ever.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Overall, THIS WAS A GREAT GREAT READ!!! YOU ALL SHOULD READ IT!!!<br><br><blockquote> <b> “The shortest distance between two points is the line from me to you.” </b> </blockquote><br>Also, check out its book trailer--&gt; <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=t5D9naNNSkI&amp;feature=youtu.be" rel="nofollow noopener">VAIN by Fisher Amelie</a><br><br><b> 5++++ DEVASTATINGLY BEAUTIFUL STARS!!! </b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <span id="freeText17586604573690735936" style="display:none"><br><b>Hello everyone!!</b><br><br><i>Who am I??<br><br>Let me tell you a bit about myself...</i><br><br><br><b>
  <i>I am cruel and unrelenting.I manipulate,use,disrespect and take advantage of every person I call friend.<br><br>If you have a boyfriend...I am your worst nightmare!<br><br><br>Everything I own is skin tight because I have a body for it,and because it always gets me what I want.I love the way boys stare.I love the way they want me.It feels powerful.<br><br>I rule my elite world.But not because I am the wealthiest.<br><br>No,I rule because I am the hottest.<br><br><br>My light gold eyes are the colour of amber and are perfect.My lashes long.I am practically flawless.<br><br>And it pisses me royally when girls try to copy me.<br><br>God!Get a clue nimrods.You'll never look like me!<br><br><br>I am VAIN...</i>
</b><br><br>----------------------------------------------------------------<br><br><i>And do you want to know something else???</i><br><br><br><b>
  <i>I am a girl whose maid pities her.<br><br>I am a girl who craves for attention and grabs it anyhow.<br><br>I am a girl whose father told her to keep up appearances and he’ll reward her handsomely,since she was fifteen.</i>
</b><br><br><br>You are right in thinking that I have many enemies.<br><br>But what you don't know is that....<br><br><b>I AM MY OWN WORST ENEMY!!</b><br><br><br><b>I am broken and alone.<br><br>But I never let anyone see me cry.</b><br><br><br><i>Bitch.Spoilt.Brat.Whore??</i><br><br><br><b>
  <i>I am SOPHIE PRICE....<br><br><br>.....And this is my story!</i>
</b><br><br>-------------------------------------------------------------<br><br><b>
  <i>Sometimes new arrangements can become that much more extraordinary....</i>
</b><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>All the rowboats in the paintings<br> They keep trying to row away<br> And the captains’ worried faces<br> Stay contorted and staring at the waves<br> They’ll keep hanging in their gold frames<br> For forever, forever and a day<br> All the rowboats in the oil paintings<br> They keep trying to row away, row away.</i>
</blockquote><br> <br>Everything changed when I arrived at Uganda to go to <b>
  <i>Masego!!</i>
</b><br><br>All I knew was that Masego was an orphanage in Uganda.<br><br>(I will leave it for you to find out how or why did I end up there.)<br><br>I met a man who smiled the largest smile I'd ever seen and I wondered what made him so happy. <br><br>Not being able to help myself I asked him why was he so happy??<br><br><i>Do you know what he said??</i><br><br><b>
  <i>"I am happy every day,Miss.I am alive and working.I have a roof.I can feed my brothers and sisters.I am very,very happy."</i>
</b><br><br><br><b>
  <i>Sarah Pringle told me once about a boy she had met.<br><br>"I can't describe him,Sophie.It was like my body knew instantly that he was mine and that I was his."</i>
</b><br><br>Now I knew what she meant.Now I understood....<br><br>....When I met with him.<br><br><br><b>Ian or Dingane.</b>A teacher and worker of Masego.<br><br><b>
  <i>For the first time I was struck dumb.What was wrong with me??I was the one who struck men dumb.</i>
</b><br><br><br>And then I met with the children of Masego...<br><br>I was overwhelmed and incredibly sad for them!<br><br>(Why?I leave that for you to find out too.)<br><br><br>There for the first time I saw the sun rising.I watched as pinks and greens,yellows and oranges danced and disappeared over the incredible landscape.<br><br><br>For the first time I let my tears fall freely.And I knew it was the only time I'd ever cried and had a genuine right to.<br><br><br>For the first time I raised my face and hands,palms up and let the rays of the sun wash over me.I discovered that sun equated happiness.It's bright and lovely existence was hope incarnate.<br><br><br><b>I learnt self-control.<br><br>I learnt I was worth more than the sex I'd defined myself with.<br><br>I learnt the joy of life.I learnt the joy of breathing.<br><br>I learnt that one can never appreciate the enormity and rareness of a fiery bliss without seeing misery.<br><br><br>And somehow....I FOUND ME!</b><br><br><br><i>Bitch.Spoilt.Brat.Whore??</i><br><br><br><b>
  <i>Who am I??</i>
</b><br><br><br><b>I am Sophie Price and I am....HAPPY!!</b><br><br><br>-------------------------------------------------------<br><br><i>
  <b>Vanity’s a debilitating affliction. You’re so absorbed in yourself it’s impossible to love anyone other than oneself, leaving you weak without realization of it. It’s quite sad. You’ve no idea what you’re missing either. You will never know real love and your life will pass you by. <br><br>But you will see. <br><br>One day you will blink and the haze will dissipate. You’ll discover that what once defined you has wilted into graying hair and wrinkled skin. Frantic, you’ll glance around yourself, in hopes of finding those you swore adored you, but all you will find is empty picture frames.</b>

<div id="review_553068361" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/553068361" />
    <a title="Emily May" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may"><img alt="Emily May" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528390751p2/4622890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/553068361?book_show_action=true">Mar 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily May" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily May" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may">Emily May</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780988812512" href="/book/show/17410382-vain">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer553068361" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6586002744827002003"><a href='http://thebookgeek.co.uk' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379777457i/368079.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>At this exact point as I'm writing this review, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16137702.Vain' title='Vain by Fisher Amelie' rel='nofollow noopener'>Vain</a> has over 5000 ratings on goodreads and an average rating of 4.46. <br/><br/><b>4.46</b><br/><br/>Which is one of the highest average ratings I've ever seen on goodreads, particularly for a book that has so many readers. I'm telling you this because I want you to appreciate what a tiny minority I am in when I say that I was really disappointed with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16137702.Vain' title='Vain by Fisher Amelie' rel='nofollow noopener'>Vain</a>. I'm going to tell you why in a second, but I think it's very important for you to know that many many people love </span>
  <span id="freeText6586002744827002003" style="display:none"><a href="http://thebookgeek.co.uk" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379777457i/368079.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>At this exact point as I'm writing this review, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16137702.Vain" title="Vain by Fisher Amelie" rel="nofollow noopener">Vain</a> has over 5000 ratings on goodreads and an average rating of 4.46. <br><br><b>4.46</b><br><br>Which is one of the highest average ratings I've ever seen on goodreads, particularly for a book that has so many readers. I'm telling you this because I want you to appreciate what a tiny minority I am in when I say that I was really disappointed with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16137702.Vain" title="Vain by Fisher Amelie" rel="nofollow noopener">Vain</a>. I'm going to tell you why in a second, but I think it's very important for you to know that many many people love this book. As soon as I added it to my shelves, I received encouraging comments from the book's fans and I was certain I would love it. I was especially looking forward to reading a book with an unlikable protagonist, it's great when an author can take a person you should hate, get you inside their head and make you care about them anyway. Sadly, that's not what I felt happened here.<br><br>I feel <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16137702.Vain" title="Vain by Fisher Amelie" rel="nofollow noopener">Vain</a> is too driven by a message which isn't incorporated subtly into the story but forced down your throat at every opportunity. It is about a spoiled, rich, selfish and bratty young woman called Sophie who gets sentenced to work in a Ugandan orphanage. Seeing these young children who feel lucky to be able to eat and get a basic education, Sophie begins to reevaluate her outlook on life, see how lucky she really is and change her ways. Personally, I don't think the change was gradual enough. This is an American girl who has been very well-educated, there is absolutely no chance whatsoever that she doesn't have an idea about how kids live in parts of Africa. Even if she'd never been to school, she would have seen those heart-breaking TV charity ads with starving children. The idea that she would arrive in Africa and be completely shocked at how these other people lived doesn't seem remotely realistic to me.<br><br>Also, I think I'm beginning to see a pattern with myself that I started to notice whilst reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8442457.Gone_Girl" title="Gone Girl by Gillian Flynn" rel="nofollow noopener">Gone Girl</a>. I like reading about unlikeable characters BUT I like reading about characters who have really suffered, who can offer some level of justification for their behaviour (or at least have some redeeming qualities) and I really don't enjoy reading about spoiled rich people feeling sorry for themselves. I know the author tries to offer up the familial tensions as a reason for why Sophie behaves the way she does, but it wasn't good enough for me. If Sophie had been male, you can bet the reaction to her would have been very different... in fact, she would be almost exactly like many male love interests that I can't stand. Rich, ridiculously good-looking, mean, manipulative, controlling, sexist, kinda racist... but everyone still obsesses over them because they're so goddamn sexy. The problem wasn't that I didn't like her, it's that I didn't care about her. At all.<br><br>This book reminds me of many other young adult romance books but with a gender role reversal. This time, all the men except Ian (or Dingane, as the orphans called him) were idiotic, slobbering, sex-obsessed fools with a collective IQ of about 10. It amazed me that Sophie considered Spencer a "true friend" because he didn't force her to have sex with him when she started crying. Well done, woooo, you're not a rapist! He still, however, kept trying to come onto her after that, even though she'd made it clear she wasn't interested. Every chance he got, his tongue was back down her throat. But he's such a good friend, people. I generally found this book to be quite sexist towards men, they are simply mindless tools to be used by the wondrous beauty that is Sophie. Even Dingane - who is supposed to be the man above all others - acknowledges that she's a nasty, spoiled brat but continues to fall for her anyway. There were sentences that, if they'd been said by a man about women, would have caused outrage.<br><br>Please bear in mind, I'm not trying to say the author shares the same attitudes and ideas as her protagonist. I appreciate that she is writing fiction and has chosen to focus on not very nice people. I am simply explaining why I found myself unable to give a damn about Sophie or anyone else. Another part of the problem is that I think the writing is rather weak. This is one where you can tell straight away that it's an indie novel and it pales in comparison to the other indie novels I've read recently and very much enjoyed. There's something about the sentence structure that doesn't flow and occasionally I found myself having to read sentences multiple times to make sense of them. I guess <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4785031.Karina_Halle" title="Karina Halle" rel="nofollow noopener">Karina Halle</a> didn't actually signify the start of my long and beautiful love affair with indie novels. Damn it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6586002744827002003" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1432795525" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1432795525" />
    <a title="A." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22324639-a"><img alt="A." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601824977p2/22324639.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1432795525?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="A." class="user" itemprop="url" name="A." href="/user/show/22324639-a">A.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=loved-it">loved-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=slooow-burn">slooow-burn</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=pov-heroine-only">pov-heroine-only</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=nah-he-s-too-sweet">nah-he-s-too-sweet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=food-for-thought">food-for-thought</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=pov-1st-person">pov-1st-person</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=she-s-all-sass-and-snark">she-s-all-sass-and-snark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=exotic-setting">exotic-setting</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22324639-a?shelf=_romance">_romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1432795525" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12420972121983171284"><b>4 Stars</b><br/><br/>This truly is an amazing and inspiring book. It had me re-examining my life, my beliefs and my values. <br/><br/>It’s a book about vanity, one of the most widespread human weaknesses. Is vanity a natural human trait or one that is brought on by society which pushes us to show off our physical appearance as if this increases our worth? I mean, I like beauty and I admire it just like every other person. And I think that there is nothing wrong with taking care of your physical appearance. But what hap</span>
  <span id="freeText12420972121983171284" style="display:none"><b>4 Stars</b><br><br>This truly is an amazing and inspiring book. It had me re-examining my life, my beliefs and my values. <br><br>It’s a book about vanity, one of the most widespread human weaknesses. Is vanity a natural human trait or one that is brought on by society which pushes us to show off our physical appearance as if this increases our worth? I mean, I like beauty and I admire it just like every other person. And I think that there is nothing wrong with taking care of your physical appearance. But what happens when you start looking at people's faces, clothes and wallets instead of their hearts and actions? Your life becomes shallow, boring and superficial. <br><br>It’s a book about second chances. Vain people are in reality very unhappy people who are hidden behind a façade. Their ugly behavior is just the result of feeling unworthy and inferior. <br><br>It’s a book about being human, loving oneself and loving others. If we were all made to live for something greater than ourselves, then our contribution to this world has to be measured by something more meaningful than the size of our wallet or the price of our clothes. This book does not only tell us a story about a transformation of a rich, spoiled brat to a humble and selfless girl but also shows us the beauty of helping others and raises our awareness that there are people on this Earth who are truly suffering.<br><br>And finally, it’s a book about finding true love. Sophie and Ian are beautiful characters and I love them with all my heart. This book teaches us to have faith and trust in affection and love and that no one can truly appreciate sincere happiness without first having known sorrow.<br><br><b>Overall rating: 4 stars</b><br><br><i>Writing style:</i> 4 stars<br><i>Story:</i> 5 stars<br><i>Flow of the story:</i> 4 stars<br><i>Character development:</i> 4 stars<br><i>Hero:</i> 4 stars<br><i>Heroine:<i> 4 stars<br><i>Secondary characters:<i> 4 stars<br><i>Tone of the book:<i> 5 stars<br><i>Emotion evoking:<i> 4 stars<br><i>Originality:</i> 4 stars<br><i>Enjoyment:</i> 4 stars<br><i>Effect on me:</i> 4 stars<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510504825i/24426022._SX540_.jpg" width='400"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"></i></i></i></i></i></i></i></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="12420972121983171284" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_492888705" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/492888705" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/492888705?book_show_action=true">Jan 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940016131375" href="/book/show/16137702-vain">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=epic-profound">epic-profound</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=powerful">powerful</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer492888705" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15887231149536819904"><b>5 Brilliant Stars!</b><br/><br/>I'm a sucker for a story with substance; one that's not afraid to show the raw, grittiness of a situation and invites you to dive deeply into its meaning. A story that can generously entertain while conveying a positive message...and I found all this and more in a book I least expected to...<i>Vain.</i><br/><br/>Meet Sophie Price — she's beautiful, rich, self-centered, and (you guessed it) unbelievably <b>vain</b>. Her parents are wealthy, powerful, and completely neglectful and cold. Her father's mai</span>
  <span id="freeText15887231149536819904" style="display:none"><b>5 Brilliant Stars!</b><br><br>I'm a sucker for a story with substance; one that's not afraid to show the raw, grittiness of a situation and invites you to dive deeply into its meaning. A story that can generously entertain while conveying a positive message...and I found all this and more in a book I least expected to...<i>Vain.</i><br><br>Meet Sophie Price — she's beautiful, rich, self-centered, and (you guessed it) unbelievably <b>vain</b>. Her parents are wealthy, powerful, and completely neglectful and cold. Her father's main concern is for Sophie to 'keep up appearances'. Sophie's inner dialogue will cause you to roll your eyes and her heartless actions will make you cringe and question just how someone could be so shallow. But one thing remains true for Sophie: she, just like everyone else, is capable of redemption--should she choose it. <br><br>I will not go into intricate plot details as the surprise of the story, although not necessarily suspenseful, is truly unique and makes for an interesting read. But I will say that Sophie is spontaneously ripped out of her element and thrown into a place where people no longer worship the ground she struts on. A place she'd normally consider as being far beneath her...but it is here where she'll discover her true self, no matter how painful or difficult that may be. <br><br>Ian, 'Dingane' is strong, caring, and dedicates his life to helping others. He knows all about people like Sophie and is determined to put that 'spoiled rich girl' in her place. While he succeeds in doing just that, he also finds Sophie's soul in the process. These two had a sizzling connection and I adored their initial 'cat and mouse' antics. <br><br><b>
  <i>How can someone bug the shit out of you so much yet simultaneously cause you to want to know them intimately with your tongue?</i>
</b><br><br>I could not have been more surprised nor inspired by Sophie's incredible transformation. Not only is this story wonderfully written but it also stands as a reminder of what's truly important in life. It is an eye-opening journey of a beautiful girl owning and mending the ugliness within. The endearing cast of characters will get inside your head and live in your heart. It's one of the unforgettable ones, and I absolutely <i>loved</i> it!<br><br><i>
  <b>Promise me you'll give it all to God and let Him decide it for you. He'll gift you no regrets.</b>
</i><br><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Romance/New Adult<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Mild steam/Sexy<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Adorable and heartwarming. Slow-building connection. <br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Realistic. Hero was charming, while heroine slowly builds her way there.<br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> Unique, inspiring, and emotional story. Huge turn-around in initial tone. <br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Fresh and engaging. Completely captivating. <br><b>▪ POV:</b> First person: Heroine <br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> None<br><b>▪	 Next Installment:</b> Separate story in the Deadly Sins' themed series. <br><b>▪ HEA? </b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412050368i/11316768.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Pretty-Words-Book-Blog/860331017317983" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12278780438853709481"><i><b>Like me?<br/>Love me?<br/>Want me?<br/>Hate me?</b><br/>Well, then darling, get in line...<br/>There's a crowd waiting for me outside<br/>See their faces?? <br/>They're dripping with hunger<br/><b>For me<br/>Me<br/>And only me...</b><br/>Love the way they want me<br/>Love the way they chant my name<br/>Love the way they can't get enough of me<br/>Haven't you guessed it, darling??<br/>I'm......</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783180.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>Vanity’s a debilitating affliction. You’re so absorbed in yourself it’s impossible to love anyone other than oneself, leaving you weak without realization of it. It’s quite sad. You’ve no</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText12278780438853709481" style="display:none"><i><b>Like me?<br>Love me?<br>Want me?<br>Hate me?</b><br>Well, then darling, get in line...<br>There's a crowd waiting for me outside<br>See their faces?? <br>They're dripping with hunger<br><b>For me<br>Me<br>And only me...</b><br>Love the way they want me<br>Love the way they chant my name<br>Love the way they can't get enough of me<br>Haven't you guessed it, darling??<br>I'm......</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783180.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>Vanity’s a debilitating affliction. You’re so absorbed in yourself it’s impossible to love anyone other than oneself, leaving you weak without realization of it. It’s quite sad. You’ve no idea what you’re missing either. You will never know real love and your life will pass you by. <br><br>But you will see.<br><br>One day you will blink and the haze will dissipate. You’ll discover that what once defined you has wilted into graying hair and wrinkled skin. Frantic, you’ll glance around yourself, in hopes of finding those you swore adored you, but all you will find is empty picture frames.</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402814ra/783181.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Sometimes in life it's so easy to judge someone, so easy to pass a verdict without knowing the truth.....<br><br><u><b>Appearances</b></u>......isn't that what strikes us first, what makes a strong impression on our mind.....<b>how someone appears to be.....<br><br>Don't judge a book by it's cover....because appearances are often deceptive.....</b></i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783182.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, meet someone I've come to know recently...<br><br><b>
  <i>She is Flawless.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783183._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>She is Cruel.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402814ra/783184.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>She is Spoilt.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783185.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>She is <u>Sophie Price</u>...</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783186._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>Everything I owned was skin tight because I had the body for it, and because it always got me what I wanted. I loved the way the boys stared. I loved the way they wanted me. It felt powerful.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783187.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>My goal in life was to rule my tiny, elite world, so I did. I manipulated, used, disrespected and took advantage of every person I called friend.I pulled and played with their puppet strings. I was the ultimate puppeteer. I was cruel and unrelenting.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783188._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>I rule this roost because I’m the most wanted by all the guys, and all the <u>girls</u> want to be my friend <u>because of it.</u>.....I was the queen of subtlety. I could play a boy like a concert violinist. I was a master of my craft.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>She steals boyfriends.....not because she <i>wants</i> them but simply because she can.... and yet none of those girls whose boyfriends she had stolen has the courage to stand up to her and say....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783189._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>I’m beautiful.....My lips were full and pink enough that I didn’t need much color....My light gold eyes were the color of amber and were perfect...I was practically flawless.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783190.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think we can safely say...<br><br><b>
  <i>She is <u>VAIN</u>....</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783191.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783192.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>I guess you really did it this time<br>Left yourself in your warpath<br>Lost your balance on a tightrope<br>Lost your mind tryin' to get it back<br><br>Wasn't it easier in your lunchbox days?<br>Always a bigger bed to crawl into<br>Wasn't it beautiful when you believed in everything<br>And everybody believed in you?</b>
</i><br><br><i>Appearances.....sometimes it's all appearances...</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783193._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>There's only a single alphabet difference between VAIN and PAIN.....Sometimes vanity is only a cover for pain.....because you're so broken, so empty inside.....</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402814ra/783194.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783195.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>I was my own worst enemy. That was my secret weakness. Rejection.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783196.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She has everything except the one thing her heart yearns for....<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Freedom is just that. Absolutely no restrictions. I abandoned myself to every whim I felt. Every want I fulfilled and every desire was quenched. I wanted for nothing.<br><br>Except attention.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783197._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, she adopts a lifestyle, an attitude to get it...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783198.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And she succeeds....she has attention...just not the usual kind....<br><br><i>
  <b>She is la fée verte....<br><blockquote>I was “the green fairy.” I flitted into your life, showed you ecstasy, and left you dependent. I did this for fun, for the hell of it, for attention. I wanted to be wanted, and my word, did they want me. Did they ever.</blockquote></b>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783199._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b><blockquote>“Keep appearances, Sophie Price, and I’ll reward you handsomely,” my father said to me starting at fifteen.</blockquote>
<br>And so she does exactly that....because sometimes in life it's easier to pretend....so much easier....<br><blockquote>Life will continue on. Everyone will continue their worship of you. Just keep up appearances. Just keep up.</blockquote></b>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402814ra/783200.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>She keeps up her barriers and doesn't let anyone in.....but she can't stop asking herself.....<b>"What is wrong with me??"</b>......</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783201.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>But life always gives you second chances....chances to turn it all around.....</b>
</i><br><br><b>
  <i>Time turns flames to embers, you'll have new Septembers<br>Everyone of us has messed up too<br>Minds change like the weather, I hope you remember<br>Today is never too late to be brand new</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783202.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And she gets a second chance at life when a series of circumstances lead her to....<br><br><i>
  <b>In this time of fear<br>When prayer so often proves in vain<br>Hope seems like the summer birds<br>Too swiftly flown away<br>Yet now I'm standing here<br>My heart so full I can't explain<br>Seeking faith and speaking words<br>I never thought I'll say<br><br>There can be miracles when you believe<br>Though hope is frail, it's hard to kill<br>Who knows what miracles you can achieve<br>When you believe, somehow you will<br>You will when you believe</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783203._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>....<b><u><i>MASEGO</i></u>......<i>“It is beautiful. It is horrifying."</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783204._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>It all starts with <b><u>Blessings</u>......</b>....with Masego....</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783205._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>There she sees nature....rugged, raw, incredibly beautiful....</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783206.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783207._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783208._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>There she meets a man....<br><br><blockquote><b>He smiled the largest smile I’d ever seen and I wondered what had made this guy so happy.<br><br>I couldn’t help myself. “You’re quite animated, and why are you so happy today?” “I am happy every day, Miss. I am alive and working. I have a roof. I can feed my brothers and sisters. I am very, very happy.”</b></blockquote>
<br><br>So, easy and simple....isn't it?</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783209._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783210._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>And it's there where she meets <b><u>him</u></b>.....<br><br><b>I've tried playing it cool<br>But when I'm looking at you<br>I can't ever be brave<br>'Cause you make my heart race<br><br>Shot me out of the sky<br>You're my kryptonite<br>You keep making me weak<br>Frozen and can't breathe</b><br><br><blockquote>“Dingane,” I repeated out loud. “What kind of name is that?” <br>“It’s Din-John-E,” a deep voice interrupted and my head shot up. <br><br><b>Struck. Speechless.</b>   <br><br>A deep, punching sensation washed over my entire body and I almost fell to my knees at the powerful impression. My breaths became labored and I fought for a clear head. A balmy, scorching but unbelievably ecstasy-ridden awareness swam through my body. An exhilarating, pleasant haze settled over me and it... <b>Burned. So. Good.</b>
</blockquote>
<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783211.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>He is Ian Aberdeen....Dingane.....Exile....</b><br><blockquote>
<b>He was the complete opposite of what I’d always imagined I’d be the most attracted to. </b>Straight black hair met his chin but was tucked behind his ears, cerulean blue eyes stared at me strangely, his full bottom lip separated from his upper lip in question. He was looking down a straight Roman nose at me and his square jaw was clenched.</blockquote>
<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783212.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She feels this way whenever he's near.....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402814ra/783213.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote><b>I’d never known a person could be this drawn to another human being, especially a complete stranger.</b></blockquote>
<br>But one of the first things that come out of her mouth....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402814ra/783214.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>!!!!!! :P<br><br>How is she going to control herself now?? She wants him....a lot!! :D Whereas all he wants is to stay away from her...<br><b><blockquote>How can someone bug the shit out of you so much yet simultaneously cause you to want to know them intimately with your tongue? He was driving me crazy.</blockquote>
<br>Oh. My. Word.</b><br><br>*shakes head* Poor, poor Sophie..... :DD<br><br>Moving on.....<br><br>There she meets <b><u>them</u></b>...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783215.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783216._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They've faced the most horrifying situations in their lives and yet their hope is alive....<br><blockquote>
<b>I’d never seen such purely happy people in my entire life.</b> They screamed with joy, jumped and dived, splashed and played with one another. They had this moment and they were ecstatic. They had this simple joy and it was free.<br><br>“And what is there to be joyful about?” I asked honestly, thinking on the images of dead children curled into themselves at the village. Another burst of silent tears streamed down. <br><br><b>“Life, Sophie. They still live. They breathe, they love each other, they find joy in the world around them for no other reason than because they are children. They are resilient. They will always rise above. Always....."</b>
</blockquote>
<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783217._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There she discovers the beauty of sun...it's eternal light....<br><b><blockquote>I'd discovered that the sun equated happiness. Its bright and lovely existence was hope incarnate. It exposed the dark, brought forth the light and showed you that no matter how strong or oppressive the night was, that it was infinitely stronger, exponentially more substantial and just because you couldn't see it with your eyes, didn't mean it wasn't still with you, that you couldn't feel it or that it wouldn't come back for you. It was stalwart and constant. It was infinite.</blockquote></b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783218.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>It's alright, just wait and see<br>Your string of lights is still bright to me<br>Oh, who you are is not where you've been<br>You're still an innocent, you're still an innocent...</b><br><br>And it's there where she discovers herself....where she chooses life, love and hope......<br><b><blockquote>“Your heart is startlingly beautiful, Sophie,” he stated after a brief moment of fixed gazes.</blockquote></b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783219._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She learns from those little representatives of happiness and simplicity and embraces life....<br><b><blockquote>No one is more aware of themselves as these children are. They have nothing, have no one but us, have seemingly no reason to be hopeful... yet they are. They choose to be happy even though the obviously easier choice would be to be frightened or sad and they have real reason to be those things as well. But they have life and faith and hope and love and they choose those things. Their innocence is addicting, their hope is catching and I’m happy to be surrounded by them.”</blockquote></b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783220.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There she falls in love.....<br><b><blockquote>My eyes closed when he pulled the bands holding both braids and they slipped off into his hands. His fingers deftly freed both plaits painfully slowly all the way to the top of my head. Finally, I felt his fingers sift through the length to the ends. <br><br>“It’s the favorite part of my day.” <br><br>My eyes opened lazily. “What do you mean?” I whispered. <br><br>“When you undo them and run your hands throughout the waves. That’s my favorite part of the day.”</blockquote></b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402814ra/783221.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><blockquote>“Thank you,” I whispered, bringing my face near his. “It’s not enough, but I have to say it. Thank you for saving my life.”</blockquote></b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397902i/768305.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><blockquote>“Feel this,” he told me before letting his fingertips flow like water over the curves of my hand laying flat on the sofa, out of sight.</blockquote></b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402814ra/783222.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><blockquote>I smiled at him and we stood quietly, our hands on one another as if we were both awakening to whatever it was that was surrounding us both then. It was written all over us. There was something practically tangible there, like a ray of sun, warming us through to our souls. You could see it, you could feel it, but you couldn’t quite capture it in your hands. That didn’t mean it wasn’t there though. Oh, it was there and it weighed a thousand delicious pounds. <br><br>I let that pressure inundate me, let it tether me to him.</blockquote></b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783223.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And he promises her.....<br><b><blockquote>“The shortest distance between two points is the line from me to you.”</blockquote></b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783224.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote><b>Soph,......I breath just to be near you ~ Ian</b></blockquote>
<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402814ra/783225.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And there their borders become her borders too....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783226.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is a story about a girl who's lost...<br>This is a story of her discovering, finding herself...<br>This is a story about finding beauty in love, life, faith amongst death, terror and despair...<br>This is a story about finding hope in the most hopeless situations<br>This is a story about finding happiness, sunshine when all you see is darkness surrounding you...<br>This is a story about a girl <b>in pain</b><br>This is a story about a girl who is <b><u>VAIN</u></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783227.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So take my hand<br>And come with me<br>On this beautiful, insane journey....<br>Here you'll find....<br><b>Vanity and vulnerability<br>Apathy and angels<br>Inhumanity and innocence<br>Nastiness and nobleness...</b><br>There'll be tears<br>And there'll be smiles<br>There'll be love<br>And there'll be life<br>But through it all don't forget what I'm<br>And if you do...<br>Well, then darling, I'll remind you again and again<br>I'm <b><u>VAIN</u></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783228.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Buh bye!! :))<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402814ra/783229.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>-----------------------------------------------------------------------<br><b><blockquote>“You may have misery,” she continued, ignoring my plea, “you may lose hope in the sorrow of an unplanned life but as long as you have faith and trust in adoration, in affection, in love, that sorrow will turn to happiness. And that is a constant, dear.” She breathed deeply and steadily for a moment, seemingly catching her breath. <br><br>“No one can know sincere happiness, Sophie, without first having known sorrow. One can never appreciate the enormity and rareness of such a fiery bliss without seeing misery, however unfair that may be...."</blockquote></b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783230.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783231._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783232._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783233._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783234._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Wish you all the colours of happiness in life, readers....and everyone else!!...Try this story...you'll find so many in there itself....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783235._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>-----------------------------------------------------------------------<br>Sophie and Ian's song.....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402814i/783236._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/473953.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></i></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer490636686" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5716269681540738739">When you see the book's title, the cover and read the blurb briefly.. What do you think??<br/><br/>That Sophie Price is a bitch? Spoilt brat? Thinks the world is in her palm or that she can buy it with her credit card? Shallow, vindictive?...<br/><b>WELL... Yes.. thats exactly how this book starts off... Sophie Price is a bitch..</b><br/><br/>Then you think that oh, she's a bitch but a hottie will walk in, sway her off her feet, they will fall in love and a bit of drama here and there then a HEA?<br/><b>Well, you've got that bit wrong</b></span>
  <span id="freeText5716269681540738739" style="display:none">When you see the book's title, the cover and read the blurb briefly.. What do you think??<br /><br />That Sophie Price is a bitch? Spoilt brat? Thinks the world is in her palm or that she can buy it with her credit card? Shallow, vindictive?...<br /><b>WELL... Yes.. thats exactly how this book starts off... Sophie Price is a bitch..</b><br /><br />Then you think that oh, she's a bitch but a hottie will walk in, sway her off her feet, they will fall in love and a bit of drama here and there then a HEA?<br /><b>Well, you've got that bit wrong..<br /><br />The story takes a totally unexpected turn, Her life changes, totally upside down!! And she can do absolutely NOTHING about it...</b><br /><br />Now we meet the new Sophie Price, Caring, loving, strong willed, earned self-esteem in her own eyes.. <b>She's HAPPY ^_^<br />She looks in the mirror and sees someone happy, someone with a genuine smile and a warm heartbeat!</b><br /><br />She's got people who love her, not my her money or appearence, but for her heart..<br />Yes, a boy does walk in, totally HOT and does sway her off her feet but the story is not what you think it is..<br /><br /><b>I loved Ian, OMG! Loveddddddddd him<br /><br />I liked Spencers character, I'd like to read his story one day! ;;)</b><br /><br />I'd say this book is a must read, an eye-opener in so many ways. This book shows us that WE CAN BREAK THE CYCLE IF WE WILL TO.<br /><br />I loved this story, it caused my eyes to leak and heart to ache a lot, but I still LOVED IT!!<br /><br /><b>Two-three things which I didn't like</b><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Some aspects of this book I didn't get, that WHY THE FUCK DIDN'T HER PARENTS EVER GIVE HER LOVE? AFFECTION? IMPORTANCE? I mean she was their only child, so why love for each other but not for her, that seemed off.. <br />And which parent in their right mind would send a child to such a place? A place which has life threatening situations, I mean.. Yes its a nice cause and stuff.. BUT I'm sorry, My parents would never send me there unless I myself wanted to go.. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Lots of faith, my love. It always works out in the end. Somehow.<br />Somehow we turn thirty beds into sixty. Somehow we stretch our food to impossible measures. Somehow we survive on our impossibly meager income. Somehow we love them all equally.<br />Somehow.”</i>
</b></span>
